!!!!!: 31 (dec). All of them are signs/billboards, except for 0x233, which is the "Sneaky guy" in Threed
#####: 1, + 10

------
DUMP
------
Exact: values are absolutely identical between games.
Partial exact: values are not absolutely identical, but simply mapped differently.
Not exact: values aren't related in any apparent way.

Exceptions:
 - Entry 0000: Direction is 04 in EB, but 00 in M2
 - Entry 00B9: Blue cow; has no flag in EB, has flag $000D in M2
 - Unaligned primary text address entries marked with !!!!!. Seriously, wtf? They're not even used.
   Don't know how to detect these yet, except that all of the guilty entries are signs, except for the Threed guy.


Type values:
  01 - Person
  02 - Item (gift box, casket, trash can, etc.)
  03 - Object

Direction values:
  00 - Up          04 - Down
  01 - Up-right    05 - Down-left
  02 - Right       06 - Left
  03 - Down-right  07 - Up-left


EB to M2:
=========
00   :00    (exact)             Type
01-02:02-03 (partial exact)     Sprite
03   :01    (exact)             Direction to face
04-05:04-05 (partial exact)     Movement value
06-07:06-07 (exact)             Flag
08   :08    (exact)             00 (items) or 01 (people/objects)
09-0C:0C-0F (not exact)         Primary text pointer
0D-10:10-13                     Secondary text pointer (people/objects; not exact) or item number (items; partial exact)

M2 to EB:
=========
00   :00    (exact)             Type
01   :03    (exact)             Direction to face
02-03:01-02 (partial exact)     Sprite
04-05:04-05 (partial exact)     Movement value
06-07:06-07 (exact)             Flag
08   :08    (exact)             00 (items) or 01 (people/objects)
{IF REGULAR ENTRY:}
  09-0B:(none?)                   Unknown. Recurring 10's and 80's; possibly status flags?
  0C-0F:09-0C (not exact)         Primary text pointer
  10-13:0D-10                     Secondary text pointer or item number
{IF UNALIGNED CRAP ENTRY:)
  09-0C:09-0C (partial exact)     Primary text pointer; not apparently used (identical values read from another table)
  0D-13:(none)                    Not used (?)
